Current Commentary

This Year

Natural and Man-Made Disasters of the Past Year

The year 1931 was truly a year of calamities for our nation. It was a year of great suffering and hardship for our common people. The torment of drought, the devastation of floods, the destruction of artillery fire, and the scourge of soldiers and bandits. South of the Yangtze River, north of the Yellow River, there were scattered bloodstains, piles of white bones, and a desolate wail, forming a tragic and horrifying picture. Was this a natural disaster or a man-made one? Was it an unavoidable apocalypse or the inevitable bitter fruit of evil deeds? If this was a man-made disaster rather than a natural one, and if this was not an unavoidable calamity, but rather a result of our own sowing of evil seeds, then we must ask: who planted these evil seeds? Who is the culprit responsible for this catastrophic calamity?

In the past year, we have suffered from various disasters, including droughts, floods, hailstorms, pests, epidemics, soldiers, and bandits. All kinds of natural and man-made disasters descended upon us simultaneously. Suiyuan, Gansu, and Shaanxi have been suffering from droughts for years, and have not yet recovered. According to newspaper reports, in Gansu, the affected areas included over sixty counties, where people could not find food and even resorted to cannibalism. At the same time, the entire region was rife with bandits. The entire cities of Minyuan, Lixian, and Zhenfan were massacred. In Wuwei, Tianning, Dinglin, Tanwu, Shantong, and Weiwu, three to four thousand people were massacred in each location. In addition, there were military disasters, with warlords forcibly conscripting soldiers, requiring the people to share the cost, averaging 200 yuan per person. Furthermore, due to a lack of military funds, the people were ordered to grow opium, forcing them to sell their wives and children to meet the demands. In total, about 1.4 million people in the province died from famine, about 600,000 died from epidemics, about 300,000 died from soldiers and bandits, and about 50,000 to 60,000 died from the earthquake in Liangzhou. In total, the number of deaths exceeded 2.4 million. In Shaanxi, there were 92 counties, suffering from a severe drought for three years, which led to widespread banditry. The types of disasters were numerous and unprecedented. The entire province was covered in thorns, and no smoke rose from the stoves. Floating corpses and remains were everywhere. In Henan, last year's war caused the most severe damage, with soldiers, bandits, floods, droughts, locusts, and hailstorms all taking their toll. The disaster area covered more than 60 counties in the province, especially Gushi, Xiping, Qixian, Queshan, Yuxian, Weishi, Xin'an, Huaxian, and Yuanwu counties, which were particularly severely affected. In Suiyuan, natural disasters have occurred frequently for the past three years, with the old and young starving to death and women displaced. The population of Suiyuan, originally 22 million, has now decreased to just over 18 million. In Qinghai, the disaster situation of soldiers, bandits, epidemics, and famine is no less severe than in Shaanxi and Gansu. Just in terms of epidemics, more than 70,000 people died in the 29 Mongol tribes, more than 90,000 people died in the Hainan people, and more than 100,000 people died in the 25 Yushu tribes. In addition, the number of deaths from other soldiers, bandits, and famine can be imagined. In Ningxia, people were besieged by soldiers and bandits, and the people died without recourse. Hundreds of thousands of disaster victims were trapped by hunger and cold. The disaster situation in the Northwest provinces has been described above, and the common disaster in the provinces of the Yangtze River basin is even more like a prairie fire, unapproachable. In Jiangxi, it has been the nest of the Communist Party for years. The Communist-controlled area covers 33 counties and one city, the semi-Communist-controlled area covers 21 counties and one city, and the area where their power is scattered covers 20 counties. The provincial government's power actually extends to less than ten counties. In Hunan, the Communist Party's power is no less than in Jiangxi. Furthermore, in Hubei, Anhui, Guangdong, Jiangsu, Fujian, Sichuan, and Yunnan, almost all provinces and regions in the country have suffered from the scourge of the Communist Party. Wherever the Communist army goes, the fields are leveled, and the houses are destroyed. Scattered troops and guerrillas appear and disappear unpredictably. Wealthy gentlemen and landlords are arbitrarily killed, further plunging the entire country into extreme terror and extreme threats. In total, the number of people in various provinces suffering from the Communist scourge is also considerable.

The central government is deeply disturbed by this hidden danger and has launched three large-scale encirclement campaigns, determined to completely eliminate it with all its strength. In the three campaigns, a total of 700,000 troops were mobilized. In the third campaign, President Chiang himself went to Jiangxi to supervise the suppression. However, unfortunately, the campaign was unsuccessful, and according to unofficial statistics, the central army suffered losses of more than 200,000, with many generals and colonels killed.

In June and July, after prolonged rain, unprecedented and severe floods suddenly occurred across the country. Wherever the floods went, people and livestock were swept away, and fields and houses were destroyed. According to statistics from the National Government Flood Relief Committee, the reported disaster areas included 11 counties in Zhejiang, 19 counties in Jiangsu, 26 counties in Anhui, 6 counties in Jiangxi, 16 counties in Hubei, 27 counties in Hunan, 15 counties in Shandong, 19 counties in Henan, and 3 counties in Shaanxi. The total number of counties was 142, the number of affected people was 44,477,443, the number of deaths was 154,655, the loss of farmland was 3,505,402 hectares, and the loss of houses was 2,554,234. However, these figures are only statistics for the reported disaster areas. In fact, the affected areas included 18 provinces and regions, and the number of disaster victims and the extent of the losses were even more countless. In addition to the above nine provinces and regions, Guangdong, Guangxi, Sichuan, Yunnan, Guizhou, Fujian, Zhili, Liaoning, and Gansu, as well as Jiangnan and Hebei, were all hit by huge waves and vast expanses of water. Wherever the floods went, everything turned into red earth, and the pitiful cries of hunger and cold could be heard everywhere. Now, with the cold weather and the end of the year, the disaster victims are suffering from hunger and cold, with no way to survive and no way to appeal. This extremely cruel scene is something we have witnessed ourselves. Is this the human world or hell? We must close our eyes and think carefully.

The central government also paid great attention to this flood. The National Government issued a decree to establish a Flood Relief Committee and issued seven orders in a row to practice thrift and use funds to relieve the disaster. On September 8, it also ordered the issuance of 80 million yuan in disaster relief bonds, planning to issue 30 million yuan in September and another 50 million yuan in December. It also planned to borrow wheat from the United States for relief. Provinces and cities also established flood relief associations and made great efforts to run and appeal. However, in reality, the 30 million yuan in disaster relief bonds were never issued, and the disaster relief surcharges have not been disbursed to this day. According to statistics from the Flood Relief Committee, as of recently, the finance group has collected a total of 668,984.775 yuan in silver dollars, 15.176 yuan in small silver coins, and 16.275 copper coins. The disaster area working group directly distributed 3,114,236 yuan to the disaster areas. Another small portion of the funds was used for sanitation work. This amount was collected from various sources and was not allocated by the government. Based on this fact, we cannot help but admit that the government has only drawn a big cake for the disaster relief work, asking the disaster victims to take it and satisfy their hunger.

In addition, there was the Korean expulsion of Chinese incident, the tragic incident of the seizure of the Northeast, and the Tianjin unrest. The losses from all kinds of disasters are even more impossible to calculate. In short, at present, when we look around our country, it is truly full of devastation. East, west, south, north, there is not a single clean piece of land. "The people suffer deeply." We cannot help but utter such a moan in this painful reality, and we cannot help but stroke the wounds all over our bodies and cry out loudly. Can this tragic moan and painful cry be blown into the ears of the party and government leaders with the wind?

The year 1931 was indeed a year of great hardship and calamity for us. However, when we reach the end of the desperate road, who dares to say that a new world will not unfold? Will China forever be a "country of famine"? Will it forever be unable to enter the realm of a "modern country"? We will never believe it. We should shout loudly, "Roar, you ancient China! Rise up, you weaklings who have fallen into the abyss of suffering! New hope will be presented to us with the year 1932."

Important Domestic Telegrams II

(Tokyo) A telegram from Tianjin states that the situation on the Panshan front of the Yingkou Line is critical. The Northeast Army is currently using armored vehicles as the front line and digging solid temporary trenches along the railway to prevent the Japanese army from advancing. The Northeast People's Self-Defense Volunteer Army telegraphed the British Embassy and other embassies on the evening of the 27th, saying, "If the Japanese army and the bandits instructed by the Japanese army come to invade, we will resolutely resist." It is expected that there will be a major battle in that area. (United Press Telegram, 28th)

(Tokyo) The Amano Brigade departed from Yingkou yesterday morning and entered Tianzhuangtai across the Liao River at 5:00 PM. The attack will begin at dawn. Also, a certain alliance here also departed for Tianzhuangtai late at night. (United Press Telegram, 28th)

(Tokyo) The method used by the Japanese army on the Yingkou-Goubangzi Railway to clear out bandits and irregular Chinese soldiers is the usual one: a swift and fierce attack to prevent the enemy from having any rest. The Japanese army began the attack at dawn this morning. The headquarters of the Domen Command, commanded by the commander of the Second Division, Domen, is located in Tianzhuangtai. According to the message submitted this afternoon, several Japanese planes carrying bombs are now assisting the mixed brigade led by Amano, advancing forward until Goubangzi. It was found that when the Japanese army attacked Ma Zhanshan's troops on the Nenjiang front two days ago, they traveled 23 miles in ten hours, fighting and advancing, regardless of hunger and cold. The same method is still used today. It is thought that the speed of the Japanese army's advance on the Goubangzi line will not be inferior to its actions within Qiqihar. According to the latest news, the Japanese army engaged in combat with irregular Chinese troops at Zhengjiatun, six kilometers northwest of Tianzhuangtai, after 10:00 AM this morning. It is reported that the Chinese army suffered heavy losses and is gradually retreating north. The Japanese have occupied Sanchaizi and Madao. (Reuters Telegram, 28th)

Japanese Army Withdraws from Faku

(Beiping) A telegram from Jinzhou states that the Japanese army in Faku withdrew on the night of the 26th due to the resistance of the local militia and headed north to Kangping. The morale in Kangping is high, and people are rising up to defend themselves. (Special Telegram, 28th)

Ma Zhanshan Cables Ping Requesting Assistance

(Beiping) Ma Zhanshan telegraphed Ping, stating that he had completed his inspection of Baiquan and returned to Haihou, where he convened meetings of military officers for several days to discuss counter-attack plans, and requested assistance with military pay and ammunition to divert the Japanese army's offensive against Jinzhou. (Special Telegram, 28th)

(Nanjing) Ma Zhanshan has sent Party Committee member Hu Huanzhang to Beijing to thank the fellow villagers' association and report to the central government on the progress of the Party army's operations and its future attitude and preparations. Hu has departed and will arrive within a few days. (Central News Agency Telegram, 28th)

Japan Covers Its Ears and Steals a Bell

Talks by Inukai Tsuyoshi

On the One Hand, Consolidating the Military's Power in Manchuria

On the Other Hand, Deceiving Various Countries with the Open Door Policy

(Oriental) Japanese Prime Minister Inukai Tsuyoshi told reporters today that even if Manchuria were given to Japan as a gift, Japan would not want to accept it, because Manchuria has a very wide border and the defense costs are extremely high. What Japan wants in Manchuria is to protect its treaty rights. Many Europeans and Americans seem to have a misunderstanding that the purpose of the Japanese army's actions west of Shenyang is quite regrettable. They do not know that Chinese soldiers and bandits are often mixed and indistinguishable, and soldiers can become bandits, and bandits can become soldiers. Reuters has learned that the Japanese government will soon publish an article reaffirming the policy of open door and equal opportunity in Manchuria. This article is a response because the US Ambassador to Japan met with Inukai Tsuyoshi on December 24 to accuse the Japanese army authorities in Shenyang of interfering with foreign business. It is said that Inukai Tsuyoshi replied at the time that the Japanese government sympathetically accepted this protest, but asked the US Ambassador to understand that the current extraordinary situation made it necessary to temporarily interfere with trade. The Japanese Prime Minister agreed to two things: (1) Japan has no intention of occupying Manchuria; (2) Japan's open door policy welcomes foreigners to participate in Manchurian affairs when normal conditions are restored. The Japanese Prime Minister also said that after peace and order are restored, the Japanese and foreigners will definitely have even greater opportunities than before. It is said that the US Ambassador had previously met with Foreign Minister Kijūrō Shidehara to protest the open door issue in Manchuria, but the issue was temporarily shelved due to the cabinet reshuffle. It is also said that the Japanese Consul General in Shenyang has declared to foreign consuls that Japan is willing to be responsible for ensuring that the temporary government of Shenyang, after its stable establishment, repays the foreign debts owed by Zhang Xueliang. Japan itself is also preparing to pay for any losses caused by the actions of the Japanese. (Reuters Telegram, 28th)

(Tokyo) The Japanese military is now determined to take a leading role in national politics related to Asia, and its plan to consolidate the military's power is underway. Some journalists believe that the appointment of Prince Kan'in Kotohito, a close relative of the Japanese Emperor, as Chief of the General Staff is the first step in the military's plan. The second step will be to seek the appointment of former Minister of the Army General Minami as the head of a new administrative agency to coordinate the steps of the Japanese in the three eastern provinces and Korea. The Japanese have long advocated this new administrative agency, the purpose of which is to prevent conflicting measures by the Governor of the Kwantung Leased Territory, the President of the South Manchuria Railway, the Governor-General of Korea, and the Commander of the Kwantung Army. Recently, the Japanese newspaper discussed Minami's new position in the three eastern provinces, saying that there is a plan to establish a Governor-General of Manchuria and Mongolia, but most knowledgeable people believe that this statement is not necessarily completely reliable, because Japan has repeatedly stated that it has no territorial ambitions. However, if we believe in the military's plan, it intends to set up an administrative agency headed by a military leader, so that the military's主張can occupy the largest force when deciding Japan's policy toward northern Asia. The military has long striven to establish a supreme authority and create a practical plan to consolidate Japan's vested interests in Manchuria and Mongolia. According to military opinion, this supreme authority should of course be under military control, because the responsibility for protecting vested interests will be borne by the military. Japanese soldiers may also be preparing for war with Russia at this time, which is also one of their considerations, because Japan's expansion of its rights and interests in northern Asia will sooner or later lead to conflict with Soviet Russia. Therefore, the military is eager to consolidate its power in the three eastern provinces and Korea as a future military deployment. The current Seiyukai cabinet seems willing to give the military more freedom, so the military's plan may succeed. It is said that Honjo has established a temporary agency in the three eastern provinces in preparation for establishing a plan to consolidate Japanese interests under military control. This temporary agency may be the forerunner of the permanent agency that Minami wants to establish in the future. (Kokumin News Agency Telegram, 28th)

Japanese Army in Eastern Provinces Increases Sharply

Totaling Between 45,000

Exceeding the Scope Permitted by the Treaty

(Shenyang) The troops from Himeji, Japan, having just arrived in Shenyang, departed for the front line today. The destination is strictly kept secret. Most of the Japanese planes stationed in Shenyang a few days ago have already left, and their new base is also kept secret. The Japanese army departing from Korea will arrive in Liaoning within one or two days. The actions of the Japanese army in southern Liaoning are always extremely secretive. Even if news of troop movements is released, the unit numbers, destinations, and purposes of departure are not disclosed. Only a few announcements have been made about the number of newly arrived reinforcements and their destinations. It is now estimated that there are between 40,000 and 50,000 Japanese troops in Manchuria. According to the treaty, the maximum number of troops stationed on the South Manchurian Railway should not exceed 15,000. (Kokumin Telegram, 28th)

Three Thousand Chinese and Japanese Soldiers Killed in the Heihe Battle

(Beiping) According to Japanese sources, 3,000 Japanese soldiers died in the Heilongjiang battle. They were all packed into hemp sacks and forced Chinese to transport them to Shenyang. When someone asked, the Japanese told them that they were beef. (Special Telegram, 28th)

Zhao Xinbo Has the Ambition to Become Governor

Jin Ao'an Is Still Under Japanese Surveillance

(Beiping) Shenyang News: Yuan Jinkai, Zhao Xinbo, and Ding Jianxiu have formed a triangular force, fighting fiercely in secret. Zhao's backer is the Japanese military, Ding's backer is the South Manchuria Railway, and Yuan is supported by Yu Chonghan. Each seizes political power. The downfall of the Diweihui and the return of Zang are all Zhao's machinations. Zang is still in transition, and Zhao Xinbo will be the future governor. Zang is completely unfree. (Special Telegram, 28th)

(Beiping) Shenyang News: Jin Ao'an is still under Japanese surveillance. The Japanese are forcing him to take over as Director of Education as a condition for restoring his freedom. Merchants in the city are prohibited from closing their doors early. Japanese military police are inspecting pedestrians more strictly. Recently, Japanese ronin, military police, and Chinese ruffians have been setting up ways to extort money everywhere. One hundred and fifty Japanese soldiers engaged in combat with bandits in Niuzhuang. All the Japanese soldiers were killed, and firearms and two small cannons were looted by the bandits. The Japanese are quite wary of the bandits. (Special Telegram, 28th)

Japanese Army Stationed in Tianjin Prepares for Live-Fire Drill

The Japanese Consul Notifies the Municipal Government

(Tianjin) The Japanese Consul in Tianjin notified the Municipal Government by telephone on the 28th, saying that the Japanese troops stationed in Tianjin would conduct a live-fire drill at Dongjuzi Saidan from the 29th to January 3rd every day, and that in the future, the Japanese troops would no longer give prior notice of target practice or drills, and that Chinese newspapers must not publish articles about Japanese troops crossing the border for target practice or drills, and that if plainclothes teams occur in the future, they must not be said to be related to Japan. (Special Telegram, 38th)

The US Government Receives Japan's Reply

Clearly Violating Its Promises

The United States Expresses Deep Dissatisfaction

The United States Will Hold a Large-Scale Pacific Maneuver Next Year

(Washington) The State Department today received Japan's reply to the US protest against the Japanese army's attack on Jinzhou. It is currently being translated and will be sent to Secretary of State Stimson's residence on Sunday afternoon. The authorities are currently refusing to discuss the Japanese reply with the press. It is said that the United States seems to be dissatisfied with the reply, as Japan has clearly refused to abide by its promises made before the League of Nations Council. It is expected here that Japan will continue to fight against the Chinese army in the three eastern provinces, regardless of the attitude of the great powers. The authorities are currently paying close attention to the latest news from the Jinzhou area, but still hope that the dispute between China and Japan over the Liaoning case can be resolved soon. According to reports, since the United States, Britain, and France protested against the Japanese army's activities near Jinzhou last week, the authorities announced that the 1932 US naval maneuver will still be held in the Pacific, not in the Atlantic. However, according to well-informed sources, this move has no political effect. (Kokumin Telegram, 27th)

(Washington) The US government received a notice from the Japanese government today that military operations in the Jinzhou area will continue. The US government remained silent, but diplomatic sources said that this document simply proves that the Japanese government intends to complete the conquest of Manchuria. (Reuters Telegram, 28th)

(Washington) Officials claimed today that the United States Navy and Air Force will conduct a large-scale exercise off the coast of Hawaii from February 6th to 11th. (Reuters Telegram, 28th)

Inukai Tsuyoshi Sends Personnel to Beijing to Visit Old Friends

Although There Were Many Conversations

It Is By No Means A Negotiation

(Nanjing) Important news: Inukai Tsuyoshi sent Kayano Nagachika to Beijing, ostensibly in a personal capacity, to visit old friends in the Kuomintang. Although there were many conversations, it was by no means a negotiation. European and American people here believe that a new path has emerged for the Northeast issue, but the party and government believe that the people are extremely strict in supervising the handling of the Northeast issue in Sino-Japanese negotiations, and it must be carefully considered before starting. (Special Telegram, 28th)

Important Domestic Telegrams III

Feng Yuxiang Will Arrive in Nanjing This Morning

He Received a Warm Welcome When Passing Through Jinan

(Nanjing) News from the Jinpu Railway Bureau: Feng Yuxiang's special train departed from Jinan at 10:00 PM on the 28th and headed south. It is expected to arrive on the 29th morning. (Special Telegram, 28th)

(Xuzhou) Feng Yuxiang's special train left Jinan at noon on the 28th and drove south. It passed through Yan at 5:00 PM and Xuzhou at 10:00 PM that night, heading for Beijing to attend the First Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee. (Special Telegram, 28th)

(Jinan) Feng Yuxiang sold his property in Beiping for 20,000 yuan to cover travel expenses for this trip. Han also made a gift. (Special Telegram, 28th)

(Jinan) The armored train from Beiping opened at 10:45 this morning to Pukou, clearing the way for Feng's special train. (Special Telegram, 28th)

(Jinan) At 11:30 PM on the 27th, Feng's special train arrived in Jinan. Han Fuju and other military and political dignitaries all went to the station to welcome him. Feng got off the train and shook hands with everyone. He first watched the station team and repeatedly said "Good." Feng said that military training is the foundation, writing well, and speaking well. Foreign devils are useless. He then took a car with Han Fuju to the provincial government, met with his old subordinates, and talked to reporters. He advocated active preparations for war and the use of force to recover lost territory externally, and sincere unity internally. He said that the First Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee will definitely have good results. He said that he was not sure how many days he would stay in Beijing. When he came to Shandong in the future, he heard that Han's training team was working very hard. When he got off the train in Dezhou, he saw that the officers and soldiers were simple and hardworking, and military training could protect the country and the local area. Because he was tired from the train ride, he decided to go south tomorrow. He said goodbye to the reporters, promising to see them again. Liu Shouzhong came with Feng. Feng wore a blue cotton padded jacket and pants, blue cloth socks, single-faced cotton shoes, a brimless felt hat, a blue cloth open coat, and a dark blue cloth waistband, with long hair and a short beard, completely peasant-like. After arriving at the provincial government, he met with his old subordinates in the Northwest Army in Han's office and asked about them with great enthusiasm. He went to bed in the office at 2:30 this morning and got up at 6:00. He originally planned to inspect the three-way army, but it was canceled due to the snow. At 10:00, Han hosted a banquet for Feng and Liu at the Pearl Spring of the provincial government, inviting Shi Yousan, Cheng Xixian, Li Shuchun, Wen Chenglie, and Wang Fangting, and Xiong Guanmin to accompany them. The meal only consisted of three hot pots, filled with vermicelli and cabbage, and eight small dishes, also only cabbage and tofu, etc. They ate yellow millet wotou, rice, and steamed buns, etc. Han also invited the reporters to attend. Feng, Han, Liu, etc. first took a photo, and then the entire group took a photo together. At 11:30, they left for the station. Han and others saw them off at the station. Feng shook hands with everyone and said goodbye before boarding the train. Just in time, a telegram from the First Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee welcomed Feng and Liu. Feng ordered Han to reply. At 11:50, the train departed south. Feng had a declaration saying, "Compatriots and comrades, for the sake of going to the national crisis together, I resolutely came to Beijing to attend the First Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee. I hereby present the specific views as follows: (1) Representatives of various civil organizations should promptly organize a National Salvation Conference to supervise all major diplomatic, domestic, and military plans during the national crisis. (2) Establish a National Defense Committee to unify military organization and military command, select elite troops, and allocate them to the front lines and important areas to implement the use of force to recover lost territory. (3) Provide comfort to the martyrs who died in the revolutionary battles of previous years and in the current resistance against Japan to encourage morale. I believe that the above three items are the urgent tasks at hand to save the country. I have already telegraphed a detailed plan to the First Congress of the Central Committee and requested a public decision. I am willing that all my compatriots and comrades in the whole country, adhering to the spirit of Sun Yat-sen's peace, struggle, and save China, work together to promote its realization. Feng Yuxiang, December 26, 2020." (Special Telegram, 28th)

(Taiyuan) Yan and Zhao telegraphed Feng and Liu on the 28th, saying that they had previously planned to jointly telegraph the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee on the case of the shooting of students by the Shanxi Provincial Party Department in Lancun, and requested the two brothers to submit it to the Congress near Beijing for joint submission. (Special Telegram, 29th)

(Xuzhou) Feng Yuxiang's special train passed through Xuzhou from Jinan at 10:00 PM on the 28th, heading for Beijing. Han Fuju sent an armored train to escort him. Those traveling with Feng included Liu Shouzhong, Li Xingzhong, and Fu Gumin. Feng sent a representative, Gao Xinya, to meet with reporters. According to reports, Feng's emergence from retirement was purely for external affairs, advocating active preparations for war and the use of force to recover lost territory. He did not intend to interfere in internal affairs, but advocated national supervision of the government. The Xuzhou National Salvation Association Promoters also sent representatives to visit Feng, asking him to propose to the First Congress of the Central Committee to quickly convene a National Salvation Conference. (Special Telegram, 28th)

Li Liejun and Others Telegraph Urging Wang and Hu to Enter Beijing

(Nanjing) Li Liejun and dozens of others jointly telegraphed Hu and Wang, urging them to come to Beijing immediately despite their illness to jointly plan national affairs and relieve the national crisis. (Special Telegram, 28th)

Jinzhou Problem Left to the National Government for Handling

Xue Duxu Expresses Sentiment

(Nanjing) Xue Duxu spoke, stating that Jinzhou is the gateway to North China. If this gateway is lost, the provinces of Peiping, Tianjin, Suiyuan, and Shanxi will have no protection. No matter how brutal the Japanese army is, it should be defended with all strength. Even if the losses are significant, it should not be spared. Only in this way can it be shown that our country still has soldiers and is not a country passively awaiting death. I proposed at the conference that the Japanese invasion of Jinzhou should be resisted. After discussion, it was only handed over to the National Government for serious handling. However, nothing has been heard about how the National Government will handle it. The attending gentlemen, regarding it as a diplomatic issue, should be united in spirit to face the national crisis. The Japanese army's attack on Jinzhou is imminent, yet some people advocated that this case should not be discussed. I do not know what their mentality is. He could not help but sigh. (Special dispatch from the 38th)

Contributing Opinions on Economic Construction

(Nanjing) According to Fudan News Agency, former National Government advisor, American Lin Bai Ke, telegraphed his friends in Nanjing from the United States yesterday, reporting that he is scheduled to depart from the United States to China in the middle of next month and will visit old friends in the North China area. It is heard that the mission of this visit is to contribute opinions and support the economic construction of our country. Although he is not an economic expert, he has considerable connections with American silver mine owners. In addition, he has sincere friendships with Hu Hanmin, Sun Ke, Zhang Ji, Wang Chonghui, and other members of the Central Committee. Therefore, after arriving in Nanjing, he will strive to supply materials and talents according to the needs of our country's economic construction. (Special dispatch from the 28th)

Jiangsu Province Business Tax Rectification Measures

(Zhenjiang) The Jiangsu Province Business Tax Rectification Measures were submitted by the Finance Department and passed by the Provincial Committee meeting. The main points are as follows: (1) The Legislative Yuan's Business Tax Law will be postponed for another year from January next year and will temporarily be handled according to the tax rates stipulated by the Ministry of Finance. (2) The tax payments for the summer, autumn, and winter seasons of the 20th year must be collected and reported within the year. (3) From next year onwards, all those who are recognized and paid by the Chamber of Commerce and guilds will be abolished and will still be directly collected by the government. (4) Each county will allocate police to assist in handling the matter. (5) The business volume and capital amount will be re-investigated in a practical manner. (6) The verification of account books, contracts, and the organization of evaluation meetings must be implemented from next year onwards. (Special dispatch from the 28th)

Foreign Important Telegrams

Gandhi Returns to Bombay

People Welcome Him With Fanatic Enthusiasm

Communists and British Army Fighting on the Border Province

Conflicts Between Hindus and Muslims in Lahore

Reuters, Bombay, 28th: Gandhi returned here today after participating in the London Indian Round Table Conference and was greatly welcomed. At the same time, a thousand Gandhi opponents demonstrated at the port with wooden sticks and black flags, later clashing with volunteers from the All-India Congress, injuring twelve people. Police arrived later, disarmed these people.

Havas, North Xia Hua, 27th: Communist leader Ge Fuhan was recently banished by the Border Province government. His party members recently contacted government troops in the Gao Hutu area, seemingly at war. Eleven communists died in the battle and fifty were injured. Local officials have taken severe measures to deal with it. Many people wearing red shirts have been arrested one after another. Judging from the current situation, the official side has an obvious advantage.

Havas, Lahore, capital of Punjab, India, 27th: When a Muslim youth was recently assassinated, conflicts broke out between Muslims and Indians during the funeral. Four people on each side were seriously injured and taken to the hospital for treatment. Some demonstrators were also slightly injured. Local officials have temporarily banned religious parades by order, and forty-five people have been arrested. Police and troops patrolled the streets separately, and the lights must be turned off at 8:00 PM. From that time until 7:00 AM the next morning, residents are not allowed to go out.

British Prime Minister Invites French Prime Minister to Discuss Reparations Issues

Reuters, Paris, 27th: According to news reported here today, British Prime Minister MacDonald has invited French Prime Minister Laval to discuss the reparations policy between the two countries in Geneva. It is heard that this meeting will be a preparatory meeting for the Hague Reparations Conference. Although the above news has not been confirmed by officials, it is generally believed to be true. Because MacDonald, after studying the report of the Basel International Committee on Germany's debt-paying ability, stated that the governments of the countries concerned should convene a meeting as soon as possible.

Reuters, Paris, 28th: It is heard that French Prime Minister Laval intends to accept British Prime Minister MacDonald's invitation to discuss financial issues with the British Prime Minister in London or Paris to prepare for the Reparations Conference. The suggestion that France and Britain should have an understanding before the official start of reparations negotiations is welcomed in financial circles here, which see it as very important. Although French Prime Minister Laval stated that he has not yet received British Prime Minister MacDonald's invitation, French and British experts have now begun to discuss the reparations issue. It is generally believed that the two prime ministers will not meet until the experts of the two countries have concluded their discussions.

Czech Blames German Tanner for Causing Trouble in the Guangtian Case

Claiming That He Was Reckless and Careless

National News Agency, Prague, 17th: The theory that a certain country's diplomatic personnel in Russian capital knew about the assassination of Japanese ambassador Hirota has been confirmed in a semi-official communiqué issued by the Czechoslovakian foreign ministry today. It is said that the diplomatic personnel was Colonel Wanake, who has served in the embassy for many years and was about to be transferred from Moscow to an important position in the capital of a certain European country. After the Czech representative in Russia was notified by the Soviet Russian Foreign Affairs Committee, he immediately began to investigate thoroughly and learned that Wanake had discussed the situation in Yuan Dong in a private conversation at a certain informal banquet, and had once made a statement that an attempt to assassinate Hirota's life might cause war disputes, etc. The communiqué also stated that Wanake's words were only a reckless slip of the tongue. After the facts were investigated and clarified, the Czech government immediately recalled Wanake and will now order him to retire. Currently, opinions in Prague on this matter vary. There is now an impression that Wanake has been wronged, because the Soviet Russian secret police heard that Wanake had made these reckless remarks and then pieced together and embellished them to achieve other kinds of effects. Apart from this reckless slip of the tongue, Wanake has always been very cautious and reliable in his official duties, and it is unlikely that he would make such a big mistake in violating diplomatic practices.

Havas, Czech Capital, 27th: According to news received in Czech Capital, Wanake has departed from Moscow and will arrive here on Tuesday. Although the matter is currently shrouded in mystery, it will eventually be clarified after receiving the secretary's report.

Newfoundland's Finances Are on the Verge of Bankruptcy

National News Agency, London, 28th: News from St. John's: Newfoundland's finances are on the verge of bankruptcy. It is expected that it will announce a temporary suspension of payments and suspend payment of interest on public bonds of 90 million yuan within days. It is said that since the negotiations to sell the Labrador region to Canada failed, the Newfoundland government's finances have reached an impasse.

British Friends Society Donates Relief Funds

Reuters, Geneva, 28th: The British Friends Society donated 250,000 pounds in British gold to the Chinese flood relief. This money, together with other donations, can be used to send an Egyptian microbiologist and several assistants to China to establish a roving laboratory and prepare vaccines and other medicines to serve in the disaster area to prevent the outbreak of epidemics. Since the League of Nations launched the fundraising for the Chinese flood disaster, countries such as France, the Netherlands, Spain, Poland, Denmark, and Sweden have provided assistance.

Russian Coking Coal Furnace Opening Ceremony

National News Agency, Moscow, 27th: Russia's coking coal furnace built in Magni Tagutsk, in the Ural Mountains, which is the largest coking coal furnace in Europe, held an opening ceremony today. The first batch of coking coal was transported to Moscow and displayed in the Industrial Museum. The furnace is part of a mining and metallurgical plant and is connected to a tar refinery and a chemical factory, which can supply the country with pigments.

Public Telegram

Telegram from Panshan: To all newspaper offices, legal entities, national elders, brothers, sisters, aunts, since the September 18th tragedy, the Japanese have occupied our cities, plundered our property, raped our women, and massacred our compatriots. Outside the South Manchurian Railway, they have ravaged thousands of miles. From Longsha in the north to the Bohai Sea in the south, the land is stained with red blood, and the flames of war light up the sky. Our Northeast people are groaning under the iron hooves of the brutal Japanese for three months now. During this period, our authorities, based on the principle of peace, did not advocate resistance. The Japanese, thinking that our country was weak and easy to deal with, defied the Kellogg-Briand Pact, violated the three resolutions of the League of Nations, and were greedy and insatiable. They used the old trick of annexing Korea and applied it to the Northeast, such as kidnapping Puyi and establishing the Maintenance Association, forcing Zang Shiyi, the puppet, to take the stage. These are clear evidence of seizing political power in the Northeast and occupying Manchuria and Mongolia. Their intentions are known to the world. Moreover, they have used local tyrants and inferior gentry in various counties to fabricate public opinion, organize autonomous associations, disrupt order, dispatch Japanese and Korean thugs, and buy off bandits to harm the local area. All these poisonous plans are nothing more than a pretext for advancing troops and implementing aggression. In the past, Ling Yinqing and Zhang Xucheng instigated chaos in western Liaoning, and Japanese participated in their troops. The Japanese supplied the salary and ammunition. Banditry was frequent on the Beining Line, which also occurred after the Japanese sent troops. However, the Dandong-Tianjin Railway, which is thousands of miles long, has not suffered any banditry. Using this to prove that their actions are at the command of the Japanese. Is it not the Japanese who instigated the bandits in the first place? Then they suppress those bandits, with planes and bombs, indiscriminately slaughtering the innocent and good. Those who are not instigated by them and are not used by them are regarded as bandits. Wherever their iron hooves go, they trample everything. The area between Bai Shan and Hei Shui has become a slaughterhouse for Japanese bandits. Besieged by rain and wind, it is no longer a human world. The authorities are trapped in Jinzhou, never daring to cross the Lei Chi River, ignoring our needs in the depths of water and fire. The public officials of the Party and the state harbor their own private opinions and engage in endless political struggles. The League of Nations, which is supposed to maintain peace, has failed to uphold justice. What are the sins of our people, who have suffered this great calamity? I ask the nations of the world, who in this situation will decide on their own? Our people knock their heads to heaven, seeking a way out, but refuse to wait for death and rise up to defend ourselves. All of us Chinese descendants will never be willing to be slaves of a conquered country. We would rather kill the enemy to death than seek completeness through humiliation. We have organized the Northeast People's Volunteer Army. Anyone who harms us will be resisted with self-defense means, vowing to resist to the death. We must not be humiliated by violence and allow others to slaughter us. Conscience compels us, and there is no turning back. We die for self-defense, we die for the country, and we die for the survival of the nation. Death has more than enough glory. We hope that the people of the country and the wise men of friendly nations will appreciate our sincerity and will not be deceived by the rumors of the Japanese about our uprising. We urgently appeal for your attention. All the members of the Northeast People's Self-Defense Volunteer Army knock and plead for forgiveness.

Important News

Central and National Government Memorial Week

Central Party Headquarters: At 9:00 AM on the 28th, the Central Party Headquarters held the sixth Dr. Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week. Attendees included Central Committee members Sun Ke, Gu Mengyu, Chen Gongbo, Zou Lu, Chen Bijun, Li Wenfan, Li Liejun, Ju Zheng, Fang Shengtao, Ma Chaojun, Chen Mingshu, Chen Guofu, Chen Lifu, Ye Chucang, He Yingqin, Shao Yuanchong, Yang Shuzhuang, Zeng Zhongming, Chen Zhongfu, Fang Zhenwu, Shang Zhen, He Yaozu, Li Zonghuang, Jiao Yitang, Fang Juehui, Zhang Daofan, Xue Dubi, and over fifty others, as well as staff members from various departments and offices, totaling approximately 600 people. Gu Mengyu presided over the ceremony. After the formalities, Ju Zheng delivered a report, stating that the recent great unity of comrades in the party was due to the influence of the five virtues of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's life: gentleness, goodness, respect, frugality, and humility. Throughout the revolutionary process, Mr. Chiang Kai-shek, Mr. Wang Jingwei, and Mr. Hu Hanmin were all able to abide by Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings and inherit his legacy, dedicating themselves to the National Revolution with a spirit of arduous sacrifice, their contributions should not be forgotten. In the future, these three leaders should unite sincerely and cooperate hand in hand to consolidate the party's center. Currently, the party feels a lack of talent, which prevents the work from being fully effective. In the future, national construction must cherish the party's talent, and those with a specific skill should be strongly protected so that they can be secure in their positions and give full play to their talents. In terms of diplomacy, Japanese Prime Minister Inukai Tsuyoshi was an old friend of Dr. Sun Yat-sen and had sympathy for the Chinese revolution. If he could abandon the traditional policy of military aggression against China, adopt a friendly and peaceful approach, and work together towards Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Pan-Asianism, it would be a blessing for both China and Japan. As for the issue of eliminating the Communist Party, relying solely on force is unlikely to be effective. In the past, when the White Wolf bandits were causing trouble, Yuan Shikai used the military forces of several provinces to suppress them for several years, but their remnants were still difficult to completely eliminate. Therefore, the fundamental solution should be to find ways to change their psychology and correct their views. On the one hand, politics should be improved to prevent the people from being driven astray by political oppression. Then, the strength of the Communist Party will naturally decrease, and eventually it can be eliminated.

National Government: At 10:00 AM on the same morning, the National Government held the Dr. Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week. Attendees included Acting Chairman Lin Sen, officials from various Yuan, ministries, and commissions such as Yu Youren, Shao Yuanchong, Shao Lizi, He Yaozu, Gao Weiyue, Zhu Lilian, and other officials and guests, totaling over 300 people. Lin Sen presided over the ceremony. After the formalities, Shao Yuanchong delivered a report, stating that this was the last memorial week of the 20th year of the Republic of China. Looking back at the achievements of the past, most of them were passive efforts. Due to the constraints of reality, few active achievements were made. The seriousness of domestic and foreign troubles this year is unprecedented. The Chinese Kuomintang, which bears the responsibility of saving the country, is determined to overcome this difficult situation, hence the unity of the whole party this time. In the future, we will concentrate all our efforts to jointly overcome national difficulties. The original manuscript is being organized.

Ma Zhanshan's Unwavering Determination

Refusing the Japanese side's compromise terms

Advising Zhang Jinghui not to take a puppet position

A Reuter's dispatch from Harbin on the 17th reported that it had been a week since the Japanese military sent personnel to Hailun to meet with General Ma Zhanshan. However, the conditions proposed by the Japanese side have only now been partially revealed. According to General Ma's personal statement to a Westerner, the conditions proposed by the Japanese were unacceptable to him because they wanted to force him to break away from Nanjing and Beiping. The Japanese stated that if this could be done, they could guarantee that Heilongjiang Province would not be invaded by Chinese troops or other foreign troops, and they could also guarantee the expulsion of all bandits. However, Ma replied that such an act would be treasonous to him and he could not discuss it. Seeing that Ma's loyalty was unwavering and could not be swayed, the Japanese returned to Harbin in disappointment and told Ma that if he could not accept these conditions, the Japanese military would consider him an enemy. However, Ma need not worry about an attack by the Japanese military before next spring. During this cold winter, soldiers cannot hold their guns, making it difficult to use troops. Currently, the cold in Heilongjiang Province is extremely severe, with the thermometer dropping to 44 degrees below zero Fahrenheit. One must wear extremely thick winter clothing and gloves to keep warm. At this time, it is difficult to use firearms. Some say that it is not difficult for the Japanese military to use airplanes to drop bombs. This idea is also incorrect. Airplanes have difficulty flying high in cold weather. Airplanes that can usually fly at an altitude of 7,000 meters cannot fly above 5,000 feet at this time. Even if they fly to an altitude of 5,000 feet, the crew members will have difficulty moving freely. Yesterday morning, a Japanese pilot took off in an airplane in Qiqihar but landed immediately because his hands were frozen stiff in the sky and he could not fly. Therefore, in this environment, it is also impossible for airplanes to drop bombs. Therefore, Ma need not worry about aerial attacks before spring. As for Ma's cavalry, they are accustomed to the cold weather of the north and can still attack the Japanese military at this time. Within the next month, they may attack the Japanese front lines. Ma's headquarters is located in Hailun, and his troops are stationed in various places, all loyal and unwavering. If they receive orders, they will immediately move out. The road from Hailun to Keshan is extremely difficult to travel. Currently, there are bandits everywhere, and even villagers often engage in robbery. Currently, the front lines of the Japanese military and Ma's troops are 50 miles apart, and travel within these 50 miles is even more dangerous. The Japanese military has fortified Qiqihar, and a large airfield has been built on the banks of the Nen River. The sheds for housing airplanes are specially constructed to withstand the cold. The propellers and engines are wrapped in canvas, and Russian-style stoves are placed inside to provide warmth. However, even with these special facilities, it still takes two hours to start the engine. Zhang Jinghui, the Chief Executive of the Special District, once met with Ma Zhanshan, wanting to persuade him to accept the Japanese conditions. It is said that Ma's loyalty is unwavering, believing that accepting the advice of a Japanese advisor would be treason. Zhang was severely reprimanded by General Ma, who also advised Zhang not to go to Heihe to be the chairman. Currently, military funds are being remitted from various parts of the world to support General Ma. Therefore, Ma's troops will definitely be able to hold their defenses at this time and can take the opportunity to harass the Japanese.

The Disaster of the Harbin-Changchun Newspaper Offices

International Cooperative Daily is suppressed and suspended

Chenguang and Northeast Daily are also shut down

Changchun Dadong Daily is forced to reorganize

The reason is that they all published anti-Japanese texts

Harbin correspondence: Among the Japanese dailies published in Harbin, the newspapers include International Cooperative Daily, Harbin Gazette, Chenguang Daily, Binjiang Times, Northeast Daily, National Gazette, Harbin News, Donghua Daily, and Dabeixin Daily. There are also small newspapers such as Noon News and Xinxin Daily. Among them, Dabeixin Daily is a purely Chinese character foreign newspaper, the Harbin Gazette is a purely official newspaper of the Chief Executive's Office, and the rest are all commercial in nature, either founded solely by individuals or jointly operated by joint ventures. The International Cooperative Daily, the Gazette, Chenguang Daily, and the National Gazette are the most popular and the oldest. After the outbreak of war in Heilongjiang Province, the International Cooperative Daily recorded in more detail. At the same time, it promoted fundraising to comfort the Heilongjiang army, which won social sympathy, and its circulation increased accordingly. However, the newspaper has recently criticized Zhao Zhongren, a traitor in Heilongjiang Province, without reservation. Zhao then secretly implemented his destructive methods. Some colleagues also jealous of the newspaper's circulation and squeezed it out. Therefore, in the past two months, the newspaper has been in the midst of storms every day. On the 10th of this month, the authorities convened a security conference, mentioned this matter, and immediately decided to seal the newspaper. Fortunately, a certain important person interceded, saying that the newspaper is the center of public opinion. Even if it is slightly wrong, in order to maintain social stability and public opinion, it should not be sealed off immediately. The proposal to seal the newspaper was thus rejected. A few days ago, the Japanese Consulate also requested the authorities to ban the newspaper on the grounds that its anti-Japanese remarks were too radical and detrimental to diplomatic relations. The authorities were struggling to find a reason to deal with it, so they decided to order the newspaper to suspend publication. However, in order to avoid criticism from foreign countries, they did not issue a formal order, but secretly instructed the Special Police Management Office to suggest that the newspaper suspend publication on its own initiative. On the 22nd of this month, the newspaper heard this news and sent personnel to the Management Office to inquire about the truth. It then decided to publish an announcement on the 23rd to suspend publication first, and at the same time dredge the authorities and resume publication. The newspaper's Feng Yuxiang, Yan Xishan, Zhao Daiwen, and Liu Shouzhong took a photo when they met at Lanchun Jinshan Middle School north of Taiyuan on the 23rd of this month (the meeting situation is seen in yesterday's newspaper).

From right to left: (1) Yan Xishan (2) Liu Shouzhong (3) Zhao Daiwen (4) Feng Yuxiang

The announcement reads: "Our newspaper is currently in a very difficult situation due to the current situation. At the same time, the printing machinery suddenly malfunctioned due to rushing to print the annual report. Therefore, it is decided to temporarily suspend publication from tomorrow. Once the printing machinery is repaired within a few days, it will be published and meet with readers again. During this period, all debts and external debts of our newspaper will still be handled as usual, and the responsible personnel will remain unchanged. In order to prevent misunderstandings from the outside world, a solemn statement is hereby made." Today, many people in Harbin sent letters to the newspaper expressing their regret. It is said that the newspaper's president, Zhang Fusheng, is currently making every effort to dredge. If the progress is smooth, it will be possible to resume publication on New Year's Day next year. However, it is expected that the tone of future comments will no longer be as strict as before. The Northeast Daily also suffered the same fate as the newspaper. It was ordered to suspend publication because it recorded news incautiously and angered the authorities. Zhao Zhongren wants to take over the newspaper and is currently planning it. Chenguang Daily was taken over by Zhang Shuping, the former person in charge of the newspaper, who was sent by Zhang Jinghui due to internal disputes. It has been published today.

Changchun correspondence: The Dadong Daily, which was founded solely by Huo Zhanyi, has been published in Changchun for five years. Although its circulation is not large, it is highly valued by the people of Changchun. In the past, the newspaper published many anti-Japanese remarks, which were hated by the Japanese side. After the fall of Changchun, the Japanese Consulate arrested its editor, Fu Pengnian, and destroyed its machinery. Under the command of the Japanese Consulate, the newspaper was forced to resume publication, and the manuscripts had to be submitted for inspection before being published, so that the newspaper became a Japanese propaganda machine. It has been three months. Recently, the Japanese side has been dissatisfied that the newspaper sometimes does not obey orders and publishes news that is not beneficial to Japan. On the 19th of this month, the Japanese Consulate suddenly sent a staff member, the Japanese Kawanishi Tadaka, to be the newspaper's advisor, and ordered the newspaper to be reorganized into the Dadong Evening News, claiming that Huo Zhanyi had dealings with the old regime and dismissing him as president. Fu Pengnian was appointed as president, and several Japanese were assigned as editors. All the important personnel of the old company were dismissed. Therefore, the newspaper has been completely transformed into a Chinese character foreign newspaper. (Evening of the 23rd)

Songjiang

The Dispute over the Suspension of the Construction of the Memorial Monument: The County Party Department previously resolved to build a Dr. Sun Yat-sen memorial monument on the site of Yueming City in Ximen, and submitted it to the Construction Department through the county, which transferred it to the Construction Bureau for design and drawing and submitted it for approval. However, this construction requires the necessary use of a part of the former camp site of the Wu family. Other sites, such as the site of Pandao Xingyu Jewelry Store, were also resolved by the county government to be exchanged for the camp site next to the Xiyuan Bathhouse. Later, the Wu family refused to accept it and petitioned the province, causing the case to be suspended for years and has not been concluded. The Dr. Sun Yat-sen memorial monument is still not under construction. Now that the Wu family has built a building by the roadside, occupying a part of the base of the city wall, Pan Wanxing, Pan Yunqing also submitted a request to the county government to assist in the construction to avoid losing their land. After receiving the report, County Magistrate Shen stated that the issue of the location of the memorial monument in this case had been submitted to the province for approval. Now that there is no instruction, how can the Wu family start construction without waiting for orders? It is very inappropriate. The Construction Bureau has been instructed to transfer a letter to the County Public Security Bureau to stop it. Wu Boyang also telegraphed the provincial government, requesting a construction permit for the people from the Construction Bureau, but was suddenly stopped by the county magistrate. Please give a quick telegram to stop it. The provincial government replied that the construction should be stopped before it is approved by the Construction Department to avoid disputes. Please be informed.

Songjin Gentry Requests to Transfer Cao Regiment Back: Songjin gentry Yin Shisheng, Liu Shiji presented a report to the Jiangsu Provincial Security Office requesting to transfer the Second Regiment headquarters back. The report roughly stated that Songjin is located by the lake and sea, a key area of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. Bandits are rampant, especially in winter. Since Cao Xiexia, the commander of the Second Regiment of the Provincial Security Infantry, was stationed in Songjiang last year, he has repeatedly annihilated major bandits and arrested chief culprits. However, on the 7th of this month, the unit suddenly received an order to move to Chongming. Most of the important officials have departed, leaving only a battalion to guard the Jinshanwei coast defense and a battalion stationed in Zhujiajiao, Qingpu. The citizens were deeply shocked and frightened. After the unit left Songjiang, although it has not been many days, incidents have occurred frequently and crises are looming. Songjiang is an important town in the east and west, with a vast territory and many bandits. Moreover, pirates are also eager to move and take the opportunity to enter. Therefore, we earnestly request that you quickly instruct Commander Cao to lead his troops back to Songjiang immediately so that they can be familiar with the situation and provide security. This is our earnest prayer.

Suzhou

Cross-country Race Changes Route: The third New Year's Day public cross-country race held at the Wuxian Public Sports Ground was originally scheduled to start from Guangji Bridge, go to Ruifeng Yarn Factory on Erma Road, and return to Guangji Bridge as the finish line. Now, because it is during the anti-Japanese period, Erma Road is close to the Japanese Concession, which may cause misunderstandings. Therefore, the route has been changed to the Gantang Bridge pier and then back to Guangji Bridge. It is also heard that more than 40 people have joined this time and are collecting prizes from all walks of life to encourage participation.

All Circles Petition to Cancel the Additional Land Price Tax: Qian Jieyi from the agricultural sector, Shi Kuihe from the Chamber of Commerce, Zhang Jianchu from the church, Dan Zhen from the asset management office, and Ding Peng from the warehouse association and other five organizations jointly presented a report to the Yuan, ministries, and government, stating that this year's flood was extremely severe. Continuing to levy additional land price taxes is beyond the people's ability. Please grant a clear order to cancel it in order to show great faith and alleviate Suzhou's difficulties.

Wuxi

Robber of Gold Ornaments Executed: At around 2:00 PM on the 26th of this month, a vagrant named Chen Yikang (also known as Li Dagang) snatched two gold rings from the Licheng Gold Shop on Main Street in the city and jumped over the city wall to outside the West Gate. He was arrested by the Fourth Branch of the Public Security Bureau and transferred to the Huishan Fifth Regiment headquarters by the County Public Security Bureau for interrogation. Yesterday, the 28th, at around 5:00 PM, Regiment Commander Liang Zuoxun sentenced him to death in accordance with the law on punishing bandits and immediately dispatched a team to escort the criminal to an open space under the train and execute him by shooting. It is heard that Chen was 20 years old and from Wuping County, Guangdong.

Seventh Branch Seizes a Large Batch of Opium: Wang Weiqing, a villager from Jiejing Port, the border area between Wu and Xi, purchased six pieces of red soil (opium) weighing fifty to sixty taels in Shanghai a few days ago. He took a boat from Shanghai to Xinqiao Port in the county and transported it into a small boat to go elsewhere. He was spotted by Wang Xicheng, the No. 3 patrol officer of the Second Team of the Sixth Water Police Team, who, together with the chief police officer of the Seventh Branch of the Public Security Bureau, went forward and seized the opium and detained Wang Weiqing. Hui Haoqian, the chief of the branch bureau, held a preliminary interrogation in court. Wang confessed that the opium was entrusted to him by a friend to bring back. After obtaining the confession, Chief Hui submitted a document yesterday along with the evidence to the County Public Security Bureau and transferred it to the court for trial. A young woman from a red pill (heroin) organization under Gu Bridge at Beizhakou outside the North Gate transported 60,000 Guo Fusheng red pills back from Shanghai yesterday. When she was passing near Lihuazhuang, she was robbed by street hooligans Dai and You, suffering a great loss. It is now heard that the young woman has prepared money to redeem the pills from Dai and others.

A Black Night Encountered by a Shipping Boat in Houtai: Houtai Town, Taibo City, in the 12th district of the county, has always had a night shipping boat traveling between the city and the countryside. The boat owner, Zou Zengfu, set sail as usual at around 7:00 PM a few days ago. Unexpectedly, when he was passing Maotang Bridge and Lijian Bridge near Meicun in the 10th district, a boat resembling a small gunboat suddenly came along and more than ten burly men jumped out, each holding a rifle and ordering the boat to stop. After more than ten burly men boarded the boat, they overturned it and searched it thoroughly for about half an hour before jumping back to their original boat with their stolen goods and fleeing quickly. After checking the losses, it was found that 576.4 yuan in silver dollars entrusted by Shen Yongyi of Houtai to Wang Yiyuan of Beidang and others had been robbed. Yesterday, a loss report was submitted to the bureau requesting an investigation.

Jiangyin

Detailed Record of the Nanjin School Board Meeting: The Jiangsu Nanjin School Board held a meeting in the reception room of the Nanjing Middle School Experimental Primary School a few days ago. Board members Wu Jingheng, Niu Yongjian, Chen Hexian, Wu Tingluan, and others attended. Wu Jingheng presided over the meeting. After Director Chen reported on the opening situation, the discussion began. (1) On the handling of the school's turmoil, it was resolved that the grievances suffered by Xue Liangshu, Zhang Xiaoru, and teachers Xue Xiaosheng, Xue Mengyuan, and Xue Ruzhong have now been clarified and the board should send a letter of apology. As for the rectification of the school's atmosphere, please ask the Education Department to be responsible for handling it. (2) On the issue of whether the board should be reorganized due to the resignation of various directors, it was resolved to amend the board's regulations to have seven executive directors to preside over daily affairs such as the election of the principal and the reorganization of school assets. All the resigning directors were unanimously sent letters of retention. (3) On the issue of appointing the chairman and executive directors, it was resolved to appoint Wu Tinglu as the chairman and economic director, and Wu Zhihui, Niu Tisheng, Sun Shufang, and Chen Gucen as the executive directors. The chairman and the representative of the Education Department and the principal of the school are the ex officio executive directors.

Disputes Erupt in Jiangyin Party Affairs: Party affairs in our county suddenly erupted in disputes yesterday (25th). In the evening, the First District Party Department convened a joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committee members of each district party department and directly subordinate branch. The executive and supervisory committee members of the Second, Third, Fourth, and Fifth District Party Departments and one directly subordinate district branch, fourteen people in total, attended. Han Qingbai presided over the meeting and discussed that since the establishment of the Jiangyin County Party Department's current committee, it has neglected its duties and misled the party, and can no longer lead Jiangyin party affairs. It was resolved to (1) organize the Jiangyin Party Affairs Improvement Association to exercise the powers of the committee, (2) deny the current executive and supervisory committee members, (3) send a letter to each lower-level party department ordering them to refuse to accept official documents from the County Executive and Supervisory Committee, (4) send a letter to the county government requesting the suspension of the County Party Department's funding, and appoint Liu Youkang, Chen Yingchen, Lu Guanzhang, Huang Bingying, Xing Jiewen, Wang Yanbin, Tang Ying, Zhao Xingyi, Tang Kesheng, Xu Zaitong, and Xu Pinshen as executive committee members. The Executive Committee meeting was opened to discuss the organizational outline. The Second District Party Department held a general meeting of party members at the County Party Department at night and resolved to (1) support the First Plenary Session of the Central Committee, (2) support the party's legitimate organization, (3) maintain the safety of the County Party Department, send representatives to the county to petition, and immediately dispatch loyal troops to be stationed in the department, (4) a small number of elements are trying to illegally disrupt the county's party affairs, please the county party department strictly stop it, and convene a county-wide party member meeting to resolve it when necessary.

Zhenjiang

Embezzlement Case of the Chief Engineer of the Highway Bureau: The case of Sun Shiqin, the former chief engineer of the Highway Bureau of the Construction Department, Shao Fengqi, the chief accountant, and eleven others embezzling public funds has been investigated and concluded by the court and a public prosecution has been filed with the Criminal Division. It is heard that Judge Yang of the Criminal Division is very cautious about this case and personally interrogated the defendants and is still studying the facts and the testimonies of each person. The date of the public trial is said to be around January 10. However, after receiving the indictment, the defendant Sun Baoqin has hired lawyer Tao Rong to prepare to defend him in court.

Each District Requests to Advance the Investigation and Release of Winter Relief Funds: The Jiangsu Flood Relief Association previously appointed Jiao Yeshan as the director of the Zhenjiang County Winter Relief Investigation and Release. Mr. Jiao has now arrived in Zhenjiang. Regarding the progress of the steps, he is consulting with the county government to coordinate the efforts. Each disaster-stricken district has submitted a report to the county, requesting to advance the investigation and release of funds. The county government has forwarded the letter to Mr. Jiao to start the process. It is found that the Zhenjiang winter relief funds were previously set by the Relief Association at 8,000 silver dollars. Mr. Jiao has requested a prompt allocation. Once received, he will work with the county government to instruct each district to send a roster of the poorest households among the disaster victims and distribute the funds equally. However, this relief fund is very small and insufficient for the large number of disaster victims in the county. The charitable organizations in Zhenjiang, such as Zhengxin Hall, Yushan Hall, Jingxinxuan Red Swastika Society, etc., have always prepared and organized the distribution of rice, porridge, winter clothing, and all kinds of poverty alleviation efforts every winter. This year, due to the large disaster area, fundraising is more difficult and they have not yet been held, which has caused great eagerness among the poor. I deeply hope that the local gentry will provide more assistance.

Tong Jiasheng's Appeal Still Upheld the Original Judgment: Tong Jiasheng, the former district chief of the Second District of the county, was sued by Yang Xiwen in court for dereliction of duty and fraud and was sentenced to one year of imprisonment. Tong refused to accept the judgment and filed an appeal. After the interrogation was completed, the judgment was still upheld.

Yangzhou

Forging Official Documents for Extortion Arrested: Meng Gao, a resident of Shaobo Town in our county, has lived in the town for many years and has some savings. A few days ago, several strangers forged official documents from the Jiangdu Police Brigade and went to extort him. After being reported by the responsible Public Security Eighth Branch, police were dispatched to arrest a suspect named Jiang. He was immediately taken to the bureau and interrogated briefly. He has now been sent to the city along with the plaintiff Meng Gao and Ma Changfa for review by the General Bureau.

Nantong

Burial of Opium and Embezzlement Case to be Investigated Thoroughly by Zhenjiang: The Nantong County Court burned opium and found 14.5 catties of counterfeit opium on the spot, and there was a shortage of more than 1,000 taels. All circles were in uproar and presented a report to the High Court for a thorough investigation. The court has sent delegates to Nantong for investigation twice, but there is still no result. The County Court has been ordered to transfer the case to the Zhenjiang District Court for a thorough investigation. The opium and documents involved in the fraud were sent to the Zhenjiang District Court on the 26th.

Red and White Pills Spread to Jiangbei: The opium ban has been relaxed in the counties of Tong, Ru, and Hai in Jiangbei, and the sale of red and white pills is particularly smooth, causing endless harm. It is also heard that there are manufacturing organizations in Tongcheng that sell to smoking dens in large numbers.

San Yu Tax Team Leader Executes Without Authorization: Li Xiezheng, the leader of the Huainan Tax Police Team stationed in Sanyu, caused trouble by investigating salt and opened fire, executing villagers without authorization, arousing public anger. He was arrested and sent to the county government and then transferred to the court for interrogation, and was held in a detention center. The team claimed that the incident was caused by salt smugglers and requested Li's release, but it was not approved. The prosecutor's office has filed a public prosecution.

Tonghai Homespun Fabric Industry in Dire Straits: This year, the Tonghai homespun fabric industry has been hit by the fall of eastern provinces. The number of fabrics sold is less than 40,000 rolls, and it is also difficult to collect accounts. Recently, various customs houses have been unable to maintain their operations, and the weaving households in the surrounding villages have also stopped weaving. The homespun fabric industry is now in a dire straits.

The Chamber of Commerce Maintains Finance: The Tongcheng silver root is extremely tight, and since the collapse of the Yongchang Lin Money Shop, silver and money industries in Shanghai have been crowding into various shops for cash, causing the financial market to collapse. All depositors, upon hearing the news, immediately withdrew their money, making it more difficult to maintain the market. The Chamber of Commerce has been urging banks and representatives of the Shanghai financial industry for days to jointly discuss the aftermath and has agreed on maintenance measures to jointly overcome the difficulties.

Investigating and Arresting Those Who Disrupt the Market: All money shops in Nantong have recently been approaching danger, and notices of clearing accounts and suspending business have been found in front of various large and small shops, causing great turmoil in the market. The Public Security Bureau found that someone was deliberately disrupting the market. These notices were posted privately in the early morning and have been strictly investigated and arrested.

Rugao

Provincial Order to Thoroughly Investigate Disputes in the Education Circle: The provincial government believes that the educational circle in this county is becoming increasingly noisy, which hinders the development of education. It has ordered County Magistrate Qian to conduct a thorough investigation, distinguish between the leaders and followers, and submit a special report within half a month without any favoritism. The Education Department also previously appointed County Magistrate Qian to serve concurrently as the Director of the Education Bureau, and he will report to the bureau within days to take over his duties.

Financial Panic and Issuance of Promissory Notes: The county's Finance Bureau believes that the fiscal resources are not strong and funds are exhausted, making it difficult to cope with the situation. During the winter solstice of the lunar calendar, it submitted a request to the county government for approval to issue 50,000 yuan in promissory notes and is now planning to continue issuing them to adjust the funds.

Wuyuan

The Tragic Situation of Wuyuan County Being Captured by Bandits. On the 7th of this month, as dawn was breaking, over a thousand bandits attacked and captured Wuyuan city. A subsequent investigation revealed that many bandits had secretly entered the city at night using ladders, lying in wait to act as internal support. As dawn approached, gunfire erupted, and the city gates were breached. The patrol guards were defeated. In the streets and alleys, members of the Bandit Suppression Vanguard Team, each carrying sharp weapons, rushed back and forth, shouting and racing. The residents were awakened from their dreams, their situation indescribable. At that moment, the garrison troops and the local defense corps rushed to the scene upon hearing the alarm, firing multiple volleys. The bandits on all sides charged forward with unstoppable force. The police and the mobilized civilians were unable to resist and retreated out of the city. Bandit squads, upon entering the county government, broke open the jail and released the prisoners. They also ordered the Vanguard Team to loot and kill indiscriminately. Before leaving, they kidnapped many laborers and even abducted the Catholic priest. The residents' losses exceeded sixty thousand yuan. The sound of mourning shook the heavens and the earth, unbearable to hear. The area was originally garrisoned by troops, but they had been transferred elsewhere, leaving the local defenses empty. County Magistrate Qi Qingchi, with foresight, had packed his luggage and taken his family to the provincial capital several days earlier, hoping to be transferred elsewhere, disregarding the lives of the local people. Now that the area has been plundered, the official documents and grain records of the government have been burned along with the county office. It is unknown what the authorities will do.

Students of middle and higher schools in Hangzhou, since the student union decided last week to resume classes and collectively set off to raise national salvation funds, had been collecting donations in this city before last Wednesday, and in other cities after Wednesday. This ended last Sunday. It is reported that the results of this fundraising were quite impressive.
